@60102  = ~Many centuries ago, a trumpet archon named Chin Yi fell in love with a mortal man in Shou Lung and swore to protect him from enemies should he ever ride to war. When that time came, however, Chin Yi's patron goddess Kwan Ying forbade her to intervene, not wishing to contribute to the bloodshed. When Chin Yi's beloved was cut down by a yuan-ti warlord, her grief was terrible and her wrath immediate: Ignoring Kwan Ying's warnings, she flew onto the battlefield and took up her beloved's katana, using the blade to cut down the warlord and all those who served him. She continued the slaughter of the yuan-ti army until Kwan Ying herself appeared before her, arms open and eyes full of sympathy. "If it will stop this slaughter, I will ease your pain and end your suffering."

"I do not wish to end my suffering," replied Chin Yi. "I wish for my fury to sound throughout the ages, now and forever." Wanting to help her servant, but not wishing to unleash such powerful fury on the world, Kwan Ying bound Chin Yi's spirit to the blade of the man she had failed to protect and then hid the weapon in a warrior's tomb. The tomb was later infiltrated and the weapon stolen, and although Chin Yi's cries could no longer be heard through the steel of the blade, her vengeance was as brutal as ever.

STATISTICS:

Combat abilities:
– Booming Thunder: Hit target must save vs. Spell or be stunned for 1 round
– Shocking Blow: 5% chance of an extra 20 electrical damage to hit target

Charge abilities:
– Lightning Strike once per day
  Damage: 10d6 electrical (Save vs. Spell for half)
  Range: 50 ft.
  Area of Effect: 1 creature

– Blindness once per day (Save vs. Spell negates)
  Range: 40 ft.
  Duration: 2 rounds
  Area of Effect: 1 creature

THAC0: +3
Damage: 1d10+3 (slashing)
Speed Factor: 1
Proficiency Type: Katana
Type: One-handed
Requires:
 6 Strength

Weight: 3《要為武士刀注入魔法並不是件容易的事。和傳統的武器不同的是，武士刀已經是一種幾近完美的戰鬥用劍。要提升它的力量往往需要獻祭，也許是瀕死的武士要祈求巫覡將他的戰鬥精神融進武士刀的精神裡。魔法武士刀的使用者必須尊重卡拉圖和使用這把劍的武士的習俗。若是不這樣做，可能會大幅降低他的運氣。

資料資料：

戰鬥能力：
-轟隆之雷：被擊中的目標必須通過對法術的豁免檢定，否則震懾1輪
-震盪打擊：5%概率額外造成20點電力傷害

充能能力：
-每天一次閃電攻擊
	傷害：10d6電力傷害（通過對法術的豁免檢定則減半）
	有效距離：50呎
	影響範圍：1個生物
	
-每天一次盲目術（通過對法術的豁免檢定則無效）
	有效距離：40呎
	持續時間：2輪
	影響範圍：1個生物

零級命中值：+3
傷害：1d10+3（揮砍）
使用速度：1
武器特長類別：武士刀
使用類別：單手
需求：
力量6

重量：3》~

@60420  = ~Sequencer spells allow the caster to store several spells in a sequencer that can be released upon any target, including the caster. The spells stored in the sequencer are cast as any other spell and can be accessed through the Special Abilities button on the main screen. It is important to note that when you choose the spells to be stored in the sequencer, they will disappear from the ones you have memorized. However, the sequencer will last until used, so the caster may rest and gain those spells back. The main use for this spell would be to allow the caster to release multiple spells upon a target very quickly in combat without the possibility of being interrupted.《法術定序術允許施法者儲藏數個法術的能量在一個法術定序單元中，然後再將魔力釋放到任何的目標上，包括施法者本人。儲存在定序能力當中的法術可以透過主遊戲畫面底下的特術能力按鍵，就像其他法術一樣施展出來。要特別注意的是，當你選定好要儲存在法術定序單元中的法術時，這些法術也會隨之從法師的記憶中消失，就像已經被施展出去一樣。然而法術定序單元卻會一直持續保留到被用掉為止，所以法師可以進行休息將法術重新記憶起來。此法術的主要功能是允許施法者可以在戰鬥中，快速地同時釋放出數個法術在同一個目標上，而不會有被中斷的危機。》~

The message continues in one of the more alien scripts. The illithids are up to something, as is typical of the race, but your being here has most likely disrupted their plans.《這張信函上有數個段落是以許多種不同的語言寫成，有些字極度陌生，連想要辨識都十分困難。

其中有個小段落是用普通語寫成：
「基地已經建立完成，滲透的工作持續進行中。潛藏者聚集了信眾，不久後我們就可以控制住整個群體的心靈……」

訊息繼續以其他的陌生語言寫下去，看來靈吸怪又一如往常，正在計劃某種陰謀。但是你的出現或許已經破壞了他們的計劃。》~

@63098  = ~Bigby's Clenched Fist
(Evocation)

Level: 8
Range: 35 ft.
Duration: 4 rounds
Casting Time: 8
Area of Effect: 1 creature
Saving Throw: Special

This spell causes a giant disembodied hand to squeeze and constrict the target once per round for up to 4 rounds. It initially smashes the target for 3d6 damage with no save, and the target is held. In the second round, the target can save vs. Paralysis at -2 to escape. If they fail to save, the hand does 4d6 damage. The following round, the target can save vs. Paralysis with no penalty. If they make the save, they are free to move, if they fail, the spell does 6d6 damage and holds them for 2 rounds. After the 4th round, the spell is finished. Magic Resistance will stop the spell.《比格拜巨力拳（聚能/塑能系）
等級：8
有效距離：施法者視線所及
持續時間：4輪
施法時間：8
影響範圍：1個生物
豁免檢定：特殊

@63158  = ~Wish
(Any School)

Level: 9
Range: Unlimited
Duration: Special
Casting Time: 5
Area of Effect: Special
Saving Throw: None

Wish is a more potent version of the Limited Wish spell. It will fulfill literally the utterance of the spellcaster. Thus, the actuality of the past, present, or future might be altered (but possibly only for the wizard unless the wording of the spell is most carefully stated) in some limited manner. Greedy desires usually end in disaster for the wisher. Lastly, the wiser the wizard, the better chance that <PRO_HESHE> will choose the right wording. Wizards with low Wisdom will more often than not meet with disaster when asking for a wish.《願望術
等級：9
有效範圍：無限
持續時間：特殊

影響範圍：特殊
豁免檢定：特殊

@63220  = ~Dragon's Breath
(Any School)

Level: 10
Range: 320 ft.
Duration: Instant
Casting Time: 3
Area of Effect: 15-ft. radius
Saving Throw: Special

This spell causes a disembodied head of a red dragon to appear and breathe fire with the strength of an adult red dragon. In addition to the enormous 20d10 fireball, the force of the dragon's breath knocks an opponent off their feet and away from the caster. The victim can save vs. Breath Weapon to take half damage and not be blown backwards. 

This spell will not harm party members.《龍息（任何學派）
等級：10
距離：施法者可見範圍
持續時間：立即
施放時間：3
影響範圍：30尺方圓
豁免檢定：特殊

@63584  = ~Comet
(Any School)

Level: 10
Range: 270 ft.
Duration: Instant
Casting Time: 3
Area of Effect: 15-ft. radius
Saving Throw: Special

This spell is a more powerful and specialized version of Meteor Swarm. A huge meteor or comet strikes the earth, damaging all enemies in its path and sending out a powerful shockwave that knocks away all foes in the area of effect. Those knocked down must save vs. Paralysis or be stunned for 3 rounds. The comet itself does 10d10 fire damage with no save.

This spell will not harm party members.《彗星術（聚能/塑能系）
等級：10
距離：90碼
持續時間：立即
施法時間：3
影響範圍：30尺半徑
豁免檢定：無

這是隕石術的加強版，施展這個法術，一個巨大的隕石或彗星會往地球來襲並且對敵人照成損害，影響範圍內的敵人將被巨石撞地所發生的能量衝擊到。受到能量衝擊的對象必須通過對麻痺的豁免檢定，否則昏迷1D4輪。彗星本身會造成10D10的傷害。

此法術不會危害到己方隊員。》~

Each round, the victims suffer 1d6 electrical damage, 1d6 fire damage, and 1d6 acid damage (Save vs. Spell for half damage). They also have a chance to be poisoned (Save vs. Death negates) in the first round.《復仇暴風

範圍：90碼
持續時間：3輪
施法時間：8

豁免檢定：特殊

所有八級以下的敵人立刻死亡，而倖存者則將受到具有酸毒的雨水和閃電所攻擊。風暴持續三輪，每一輪中受害者將遭受1D6的電擊傷害、1D6的火焰傷害、以及1D6的強酸傷害（通過對法術的豁免則傷害值減半）。他們也可能在第一輪時中毒（死亡豁免檢定）。》~

@64319  = ~Chaos Shield《混亂護罩*》~
@64320  = ~Chaos Shield
(Abjuration)

Level: 2
Range: 0
Duration: 5 rounds + 1 turn/5 levels
Casting Time: 2
Area of Effect: The caster
Saving Throw: None

Chaos Shield increases a Wild Mage's chance to gain a favorable result when a Wild Surge occurs. Every time a roll is made on the Wild Surge chart, an extra 15 is added to the dice roll. When Nahal's Reckless Dweomer is cast, the bonus from Chaos Shield stacks with the Wild Mage's level bonus.《混亂護罩*（防護系）
等級：2
有效距離：0
持續時間：5輪+10輪/5等級
施法時間：2
影響範圍：施法者
豁免檢定：無

(Necromancy)

Level: 7
Sphere: Necromantic
Range: 30 ft.
Duration: Permanent
Casting Time: 2
Area of Effect: Up to 5 party members
Saving Throw: None

A more powerful version of Raise Dead, this spell brings up to 5 party members back to life and heals 3d10+1 Hit Points per level of the caster. They can regain the rest of their Hit Points by natural healing or curative magic. This spell restores life to dwarves, gnomes, half-elves, halflings, elves, half-orcs, and humans.《集體死者復活（死靈系）
等級：神授
領域：死靈
範圍：施法者視線範圍內
持續時間：永久
施法時間：2
影響範圍：最多不超過五個隊友
豁免檢定：特殊
